				<script type="text/javascript">
					(function($) {
						$('#edition_nav, #region_nav')
							.click(function(){
								$(this).toggleClass('edition_nav_selected');
							})
							.mouseleave(function(){
								var e = $(this),
									t = e.data('timer');
								t && clearTimeout(t);
								t = setTimeout(function(){
									e.hasClass('edition_nav_selected') && e.removeClass('edition_nav_selected')
								}, 1000);
								e.data('timer', t);
							})
							.mouseenter(function(){
								var t = $(this).data('timer');
								t && clearTimeout(t);
							});
					})(jQuery);
				</script>

                <h2><a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.ca/steve-morgan/canada-pharmacare-4-reasons_b_16489086.html" style="line-height:18px !important;font-weight: bold;font-size: 16px;font-family: arial;color: #1A1A1A;">4 Reasons Canada Needs Universal Pharmacare Now</a></h2>
                <div class="green_entry_bar"></div>
			</div>

			<div class="clear"></div>
											 											
							<div class="image_wrapper relative" style="width: 300px;float:left">
								<a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.ca/steve-morgan/canada-pharmacare-4-reasons_b_16489086.html">
									<img src="http://i.huffpost.com/gen/5288982/images/n-CANADA-PHARMACEUTICAL-medium.jpg" alt="Canada Pharmaceutical" />
								</a>
								<span class="absolute image-credit arial_11">Cecilie_Arcurs via Getty Images</span>
							</div>						
				 
			
													<p>Several national commissions on Canada's health care system have recommended adding prescription drugs to our publicly funded universal medicare system. No federal government has ever acted on those recommendations. Not yet, anyhow. By creating 'pharmacare-junior,' Premier Wynne and Minister Hoskins are in essence calling on the federal government to help finish the job and create a pharmacare program for all Canadians of all ages.</p>

            <div class="blogger_img">

                <div class="green_entry_bar"></div>
			</div>

			<div class="clear"></div>
											 											
							<div class="image_wrapper relative" style="width: 300px;float:left">

													<p>A simple Google search of "political promises in Canadian real estate market" gives you an idea of where our minds are at this election. The sentiment is pretty clear.
